# Policy Form Provisions

### Policy form clauses

| | |
| :--- | :--- |
| **CG 00 01 01 24 - LIMITATION**<br><br>**Classification And Territory Limitation**<br>The Mercantile - food or beverage stores operation applies at Location 1, class 10010, territory 003 only when the declarations show the same exposure basis.<br><br>Applies within Location 1, class 10010, territory 003; location 1; class 10010; limit $1,000,000; deductible . Classification: Mercantile - food or beverage stores; Exclusion Name: PFAS Exclusion; Form Title: Commercial General Liability Coverage Form; Limit Type: Each Occurrence; Territory: 003 | **CG 20 10 04 13 - CONDITION**<br><br>**Additional Insured Contract Gate**<br>Additional insured status for Location 2, class 41670, territory 007 applies only when the contract requirement and attached form CG 20 10 are both satisfied.<br><br>Applies within Location 2, class 41670, territory 007; location 2; class 41670; limit $2,000,000; deductible . Classification: Restaurants - with sales of alcoholic beverages; Exclusion Name: Silica or Silica-Related Dust Exclusion; Form Title: Additional Insured - Owners, Lessees or Contractors; Limit Type: General Aggregate; Territory: 007 |
| **CG 00 01 01 24 - CONDITION**<br><br>**Aggregate Limit Application**<br>The Each Occurrence limit of $1,000,000 applies with the Commercial General Liability coverage part and does not increase another aggregate.<br><br>Applies within Location 1, class 10010, territory 003; location 1; class 10010; limit $1,000,000; deductible . Classification: Mercantile - food or beverage stores; Exclusion Name: PFAS Exclusion; Form Title: Commercial General Liability Coverage Form; Limit Type: Each Occurrence; Territory: 003 | **CG 20 10 04 13 - EXCLUSION**<br><br>**Exclusion And Endorsement Priority**<br>The Silica or Silica-Related Dust Exclusion provision and form CG 20 10 edition 04 13 control before any conflicting summary entry for Location 2, class 41670, territory 007.<br><br>Applies within Location 2, class 41670, territory 007; location 2; class 41670; limit $2,000,000; deductible . Classification: Restaurants - with sales of alcoholic beverages; Exclusion Name: Silica or Silica-Related Dust Exclusion; Form Title: Additional Insured - Owners, Lessees or Contractors; Limit Type: General Aggregate; Territory: 007 |
| **CG 00 01 01 24 - CONDITION**<br><br>**Additional Insured Contract Gate**<br>Additional insured status for Location 1, class 10010, territory 003 applies only when the contract requirement and attached form CG 00 01 are both satisfied.<br><br>Applies within Location 1, class 10010, territory 003; location 1; class 10010; limit $1,000,000; deductible . Classification: Mercantile - food or beverage stores; Exclusion Name: PFAS Exclusion; Form Title: Commercial General Liability Coverage Form; Limit Type: Each Occurrence; Territory: 003 | **CG 20 37 12 19 - LIMITATION**<br><br>**Classification And Territory Limitation**<br>The Contractors - subcontracted work operation applies at Location 3, class 16916, territory 007 only when the declarations show the same exposure basis.<br><br>Applies within Location 3, class 16916, territory 007; location 3; class 16916; limit $2,000,000; deductible . Classification: Contractors - subcontracted work; Exclusion Name: Data Privacy Violation Exclusion; Form Title: Additional Insured - Completed Operations; Limit Type: Products-Completed Operations Aggregate; Territory: 007 |
| **CG 00 01 01 24 - EXCLUSION**<br><br>**Exclusion And Endorsement Priority**<br>The PFAS Exclusion provision and form CG 00 01 edition 01 24 control before any conflicting summary entry for Location 1, class 10010, territory 003.<br><br>Applies within Location 1, class 10010, territory 003; location 1; class 10010; limit $1,000,000; deductible . Classification: Mercantile - food or beverage stores; Exclusion Name: PFAS Exclusion; Form Title: Commercial General Liability Coverage Form; Limit Type: Each Occurrence; Territory: 003 | **CG 20 37 12 19 - CONDITION**<br><br>**Aggregate Limit Application**<br>The Products-Completed Operations Aggregate limit of $2,000,000 applies with the Commercial General Liability coverage part and does not increase another aggregate.<br><br>Applies within Location 3, class 16916, territory 007; location 3; class 16916; limit $2,000,000; deductible . Classification: Contractors - subcontracted work; Exclusion Name: Data Privacy Violation Exclusion; Form Title: Additional Insured - Completed Operations; Limit Type: Products-Completed Operations Aggregate; Territory: 007 |
| **CG 20 10 04 13 - LIMITATION**<br><br>**Classification And Territory Limitation**<br>The Restaurants - with sales of alcoholic beverages operation applies at Location 2, class 41670, territory 007 only when the declarations show the same exposure basis.<br><br>Applies within Location 2, class 41670, territory 007; location 2; class 41670; limit $2,000,000; deductible . Classification: Restaurants - with sales of alcoholic beverages; Exclusion Name: Silica or Silica-Related Dust Exclusion; Form Title: Additional Insured - Owners, Lessees or Contractors; Limit Type: General Aggregate; Territory: 007 | **CG 20 37 12 19 - CONDITION**<br><br>**Additional Insured Contract Gate**<br>Additional insured status for Location 3, class 16916, territory 007 applies only when the contract requirement and attached form CG 20 37 are both satisfied.<br><br>Applies within Location 3, class 16916, territory 007; location 3; class 16916; limit $2,000,000; deductible . # Policy Form Provisions

### Policy form clauses

***

**CG 24 04 01 24 - LIMITATION**

**Classification And Territory Limitation**
The Concrete construction operation applies at Location 4, class 91560, territory 003 only when the declarations show the same exposure basis.

Applies within Location 4, class 91560, territory 003; location 4; class 91560; limit $1,000,000; deductible . Classification: Concrete construction; Exclusion Name: Data Privacy Violation Exclusion; Form Title: Waiver of Transfer of Rights of Recovery; Limit Type: Personal and Advertising Injury; Territory: 003

***

**CG 24 04 01 24 - CONDITION**

**Aggregate Limit Application**
The Personal and Advertising Injury limit of $1,000,000 applies with the Commercial General Liability coverage part and does not increase another aggregate.

Applies within Location 4, class 91560, territory 003; location 4; class 91560; limit $1,000,000; deductible . Classification: Concrete construction; Exclusion Name: Data Privacy Violation Exclusion; Form Title: Waiver of Transfer of Rights of Recovery; Limit Type: Personal and Advertising Injury; Territory: 003

***

**CG 24 04 01 24 - CONDITION**

**Additional Insured Contract Gate**
Additional insured status for Location 4, class 91560, territory 003 applies only when the contract requirement and attached form CG 24 04 are both satisfied.

Applies within Location 4, class 91560, territory 003; location 4; class 91560; limit $1,000,000; deductible . Classification: Concrete construction; Exclusion Name: Data Privacy Violation Exclusion; Form Title: Waiver of Transfer of Rights of Recovery; Limit Type: Personal and Advertising Injury; Territory: 003

***

**CG 24 04 01 24 - EXCLUSION**

**Exclusion And Endorsement Priority**
The Data Privacy Violation Exclusion provision and form CG 24 04 edition 01 24 control before any conflicting summary entry for Location 4, class 91560, territory 003.

Applies within Location 4, class 91560, territory 003; location 4; class 91560; limit $1,000,000; deductible . Classification: Concrete construction; Exclusion Name: Data Privacy Violation Exclusion; Form Title: Waiver of Transfer of Rights of Recovery; Limit Type: Personal and Advertising Injury; Territory: 003

***
